 MySQL  localhost:3306 ssl  boats  SQL > with sailors_age_group as (select s.age, count(*) as total_sailors_by_age_group from sailors s where s.age >= 31 and s.age <= 39 group by s.age having total_sailors_by_age_group > 30)
                                      -> select s.age, avg(s.rating) from sailors s
                                      -> where s.age in (select age from sailors_age_group)
                                      -> group by s.age;
